style="opacity:0;transform:translateX(0rem) translateY(0rem) scale(1) translateZ(0)"><div class="ppcmsnodeweb-tmvyzy"><div class="text-group text-group-alignment-start accordion-headline" style="opacity:0;transform:translateX(0.75px) translateY(0.75px) scale(1) translateZ(0)"><div style="opacity:0;transform:translateX(0.75rem) translateY(0.75rem) scale(1) translateZ(0)"><h2 class="text-group-headline heading-text-style heading-text-size-headline-4">Frequently asked questions</h2>
</div></div></div><div class="ppcmsnodeweb-tmvyzy"><div class="accordion-item"><h3 class="accordion-item-heading"><button type="button" class="accordion-item-headline" id="accordion-row1" aria-controls="accordion-content1" aria-expanded="true" data-pa-click="{&quot;link&quot;:&quot;accordionItemHeader-Primary-What is Fastlane by PayPal?&quot;,&quot;event_name&quot;:&quot;enterprise_button_cta_clicked&quot;}"><span class="accordion-item-headline-container"><span class="accordion-item-headline-text-container"><span class="accordion-item-headline-text heading-text-style heading-text-size-title">What is Fastlane by PayPal?</span>
</span><span class="accordion-item-icon accordion-item-icon-theme-white"><span class="ppcmsnodeweb-1bk0n6-svg-size_md" data-ppui-info="icons_8.24.1__7.46.3" aria-hidden="true" data-ppui="true"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" fill="currentColor" viewBox="0 0 24 24" width="1em" height="1em" data-ppui="true"><path d="M13 5a1 1 0 1 0-2 0v6H5a1 1 0 1 0 0 2h6v6a1 1 0 1 0 2 0v-6h6a1 1 0 1 0 0-2h-6V5z" data-ppui="true"></path></svg></span></span></span></button></h3><div id="accordion-content1" aria-labelledby="accordion-row1" role="region" style="height:0px;opacity:0;display:none"><p class="body-text-style body-text-size-body">Fastlane by PayPal is a high-speed checkout solution that lets integrated merchants use our network vault to recognize guest shoppers earlier and access their saved checkout credentials without a password.</p>
</div></div><div class="accordion-item"><h3 class="accordion-item-heading"><button type="button" class="accordion-item-headline" id="accordion-row2" aria-controls="accordion-content2" aria-expanded="false" data-pa-click="{&quot;link&quot;:&quot;accordionItemHeader-Primary-Does Fastlane by PayPal affect the normal Pay with PayPal purchase experience?&quot;,&quot;event_name&quot;:&quot;enterprise_button_cta_clicked&quot;}"><span class="accordion-item-headline-container"><span class="accordion-item-headline-text-container"><span class="accordion-item-headline-text heading-text-style heading-text-size-title">Does Fastlane by PayPal affect the normal Pay with PayPal purchase experience?</span>
</span><span class="accordion-item-icon accordion-item-icon-theme-white"><span class="ppcmsnodeweb-1bk0n6-svg-size_md" data-ppui-info="icons_8.24.1__7.46.3" aria-hidden="true" data-ppui="true"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" fill="currentColor" viewBox="0 0 24 24" width="1em" height="1em" data-ppui="true"><path d="M13 5a1 1 0 1 0-2 0v6H5a1 1 0 1 0 0 2h6v6a1 1 0 1 0 2 0v-6h6a1 1 0 1 0 0-2h-6V5z" data-ppui="true"></path></svg></span></span></span></button></h3><div id="accordion-content2" aria-labelledby="accordion-row2" role="region" style="height:0px;opacity:0;display:none"><p class="body-text-style body-text-size-body">Fastlane doesn’t affect the PayPal button flow. However, you may be required to update or adjust your existing PayPal integration.</p>
<p class="body-text-style body-text-size-body"><span>Not processing payments with PayPal yet? </span><a href="https://www.paypal.com/us/business/accept-payments" target="_self" rel="" class="html-text-renderer-link" data-pa-click="{&quot;link&quot;:&quot;Accordion-Link-Paragraph-Learn more about our payment solutions&quot;,&quot;event_name&quot;:&quot;enterprise_text_link_clicked&quot;}">Learn more about our payment solutions</a><span>.</span></p>
</div></div><div class="accordion-item"><h3 class="accordion-item-heading"><button type="button" class="accordion-item-headline" id="accordion-row3" aria-controls="accordion-content3" aria-expanded="false" data-pa-click="{&quot;link&quot;:&quot;accordionItemHeader-Primary-What&#x27;s the integration effort for my business?&quot;,&quot;event_name&quot;:&quot;enterprise_button_cta_clicked&quot;}"><span class="accordion-item-headline-container"><span class="accordion-item-headline-text-container"><span class="accordion-item-headline-text heading-text-style heading-text-size-title">What's the integration effort for my business?</span>
</span><span class="accordion-item-icon accordion-item-icon-theme-white"><span class="ppcmsnodeweb-1bk0n6-svg-size_md" data-ppui-info="icons_8.24.1__7.46.3" aria-hidden="true" data-ppui="true"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" fill="currentColor" viewBox="0 0 24 24" width="1em" height="1em" data-ppui="true"><path d="M13 5a1 1 0 1 0-2 0v6H5a1 1 0 1 0 0 2h6v6a1 1 0 1 0 2 0v-6h6a1 1 0 1 0 0-2h-6V5z" data-ppui="true"></path></svg></span></span></span></button></h3><div id="accordion-content3" aria-labelledby="accordion-row3" role="region" style="height:0px;opacity:0;display:none"><p class="body-text-style body-text-size-body"><span>Since Fastlane leverages our existing payment processing systems, merchants who currently process payments with </span><a href="https://www.paypal.com/us/enterprise/payment-processing" target="_self" rel="" class="html-text-renderer-link" data-pa-click="{&quot;link&quot;:&quot;Accordion-Link-Paragraph-Enterprise Payments&quot;,&quot;event_name&quot;:&quot;enterprise_text_link_clicked&quot;}">Enterprise Payments</a><span> or </span><a href="https://www.paypal.com/us/business/accept-payments/checkout" target="_self" rel="" class="html-text-renderer-link" data-pa-click="{&quot;link&quot;:&quot;Accordion-Link-Paragraph-Expanded Checkout&quot;,&quot;event_name&quot;:&quot;enterprise_text_link_clicked&quot;}">Expanded Checkout</a><span> won’t need to make changes to their back-end integration. They'll only need to make small, front-end updates to their checkout flows.</span></p>
<p class="body-text-style body-text-size-body"><span>On custom websites, Fastlane can be integrated in as little as 2-4 weeks. Small businesses offering PayPal through a partner eCommerce platform can enable Fastlane in as little as one step. </span><a href="http://developer.paypal.com/community/fastlane" target="_self" rel="" class="html-text-renderer-link" data-pa-click="{&quot;link&quot;:&quot;Accordion-Link-Paragraph-Learn more about integrating Fastlane&quot;,&quot;event_name&quot;:&quot;enterprise_text_link_clicked&quot;}">Learn more about integrating Fastlane</a><span>.</span></p>
</div></div><div class="accordion-item"><h3 class="accordion-item-heading"><button type="button" class="accordion-item-headline" id="accordion-row4" aria-controls="accordion-content4" aria-expanded="false" data-pa-click="{&quot;link&quot;:&quot;accordionItemHeader-Primary-What will my customers experience?&quot;,&quot;event_name&quot;:&quot;enterprise_button_cta_clicked&quot;}"><span class="accordion-item-headline-container"><span class="accordion-item-headline-text-container"><span class="accordion-item-headline-text heading-text-style heading-text-size-title">What will my customers experience?</span>
</span><span class="accordion-item-icon accordion-item-icon-theme-white"><span class="ppcmsnodeweb-1bk0n6-svg-size_md" data-ppui-info="icons_8.24.1__7.46.3" aria-hidden="true" data-ppui="true"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" fill="currentColor" viewBox="0 0 24 24" width="1em" height="1em" data-ppui="true"><path d="M13 5a1 1 0 1 0-2 0v6H5a1 1 0 1 0 0 2h6v6a1 1 0 1 0 2 0v-6h6a1 1 0 1 0 0-2h-6V5z" data-ppui="true"></path></svg></span></span></span></button></h3><div id="accordion-content4" aria-labelledby="accordion-row4" role="region" style="height:0px;opacity:0;display:none"><p class="body-text-style body-text-size-body"><span>Customers can create a Fastlane profile during the traditional guest checkout process. Next time they shop, they'll provide an email for passwordless login and we'll autofill their payment and shipping details for faster checkout. </span><a href="https://www.paypal.com/us/fastlane" target="_self" rel="" class="html-text-renderer-link" data-pa-click="{&quot;link&quot;:&quot;Accordion-Link-Paragraph-Learn more about the Fastlane shopping experience&quot;,&quot;event_name&quot;:&quot;enterprise_text_link_clicked&quot;}">Learn more about the Fastlane shopping experience</a><span>.</span></p>
</div></div><div class="accordion-item"><h3 class="accordion-item-heading"><button type="button" class="accordion-item-headline" id="accordion-row5" aria-controls="accordion-content5" aria-expanded="false" data-pa-click="{&quot;link&quot;:&quot;accordionItemHeader-Primary-Where is Fastlane available?&quot;,&quot;event_name&quot;:&quot;enterprise_button_cta_clicked&quot;}"><span class="accordion-item-headline-container"><span class="accordion-item-headline-text-container"><span class="accordion-item-headline-text heading-text-style heading-text-size-title">Where is Fastlane available?</span>
</span><span class="accordion-item-icon accordion-item-icon-theme-white"><span class="ppcmsnodeweb-1bk0n6-svg-size_md" data-ppui-info="icons_8.24.1__7.46.3" aria-hidden="true" data-ppui="true"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" fill="currentColor" viewBox="0 0 24 24" width="1em" height="1em" data-ppui="true"><path d="M13 5a1 1 0 1 0-2 0v6H5a1 1 0 1 0 0 2h6v6a1 1 0 1 0 2 0v-6h6a1 1 0 1 0 0-2h-6V5z" data-ppui="true"></path></svg></span></span></span></button></h3><div id="accordion-content5" aria-labelledby="accordion-row5" role="region" style="height:0px;opacity:0;display:none"><p class="body-text-style body-text-size-body">Fastlane is currently available in the US only and is coming to other markets later in 2025.</p>
</div></div></div></section><!--/$--><!--$--><section class="article-card-template not-mounted section-wrapper neutral-100-plate grid ppe ppe-palette grid-compact ppcmsnodeweb-4tets9"><div class="ppcmsnodeweb-y59vw7"><div class="text-group text-group-alignment-start article-card-template-header" style="opacity:0;transform:translateX(0.75px) translateY(0.75px) scale(1) translateZ(0)"><div style="opacity:0;transform:translateX(0.75rem) translateY(0.75rem) scale(1) translateZ(0)"><h2 class="text-group-headline heading-text-style heading-text-size-headline-4">Get smarter.
